<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдумывать.html>выду́мывать</a> (8565)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдумать.html>вы́думать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výdumatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдумывать.html>выду́мывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vydúmyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдумать.html>вы́думать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to invent, to contrive, to devise</li>
<li>to concoct, to fabricate, to make up</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выдыхать.html>выдыха́ть</a> (19486)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ды́хать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dýxatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдыхать.html>выдыха́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vydyxátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выдохнуть.html>вы́дохнуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to breathe out, to exhale</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́езд</a> (4716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vyjezžátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognates include <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">výjezd</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́езд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výjezd</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́езда</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́езды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезд.html>вы́ездов</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выездной.html>выездно́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>departure, leaving</li>
<li>exit, egress; gateway</li>
<li>exit road</li>
<li>emigration</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a> (5390)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating action or motion out of an area</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-езжа́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jezžátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyjezžátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выехать.html>вы́ехать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exit (by vehicle)</li>
<li>to break in (a horse)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">вы́ездить</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">výjezditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***выесть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выесть.html>вы́есть</a> (24372)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>есть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jestʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выесть.html>вы́есть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výjestʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">выеда́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to eat away <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to erode or corrode gradually</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>, to eat out (eat the inside)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b>вы́еденного</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:яйцо.html>яйца́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стоять.html>сто́ит</a></i> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">idiomatic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výjedennovo</b> jajcá ne stóit</i> ― <span class="e-translation">not worth a hill of beans, not worth twopence, not worth of a brass farthing</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">not worth an eaten out egg</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:съесть.html>съесть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:внутренний.html>вну́треннюю</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:часть.html>часть</a> чего-нибудь <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:выесть.html>Вы́есть</a></span> <a href = vnd.unilang:начинка.html>начи́нку</a>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><a href = vnd.unilang:разрушить.html>разру́шить</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:вытравить.html>вы́травить</a> чем-нибудь <a href = vnd.unilang:едкий.html>е́дким</a> <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>Ды́мом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза</a> <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:выесть.html>вы́ело</a></span>. </span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выехать.html>вы́ехать</a> (2836)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">indicating action or motion out of an area</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ехать.html>е́хать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">jéxatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to go (by vehicle)</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выехать.html>вы́ехать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výjexatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выезжать.html>выезжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to exit (by vehicle)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжавший.html>вы́жавший</a> (9868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a> (9868)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жать.html>жать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to press, to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výžatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze out, to press out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>сок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лимон.html>лимо́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výžatʹ</b> sok iz limóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">squeeze juice out of a lemon</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wring (a cloth, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wring out, to get out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výžatʹ</b> vsjó vozmóžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the most</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:максимальный.html>максима́льную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výžatʹ</b> maksimálʹnuju skórostʹ iz avtomobílja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the most mileage out of one's car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:информация.html>информа́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výžatʹ</b> informáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wring information</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>výžatʹ</b> iz sebjá ulýbku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to force a smile</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press, to lift (a weight)</li>
<li>to step on, to press on (the clutch, etc.)</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ждать.html>ждать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ždatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжечь.html>вы́жечь</a> (10552)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жечь.html>жечь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žečʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжечь.html>вы́жечь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výžečʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burn out, to burn down, to scorch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клеймо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžigátʹ</b> klejmó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to brand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́реву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžigátʹ</b> po dérevu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do poker-work, to do pyrography</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cauterize</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выживать.html>выжива́ть</a> (15494)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжить.html>вы́жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">výžitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выживать.html>выжива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyživátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжить.html>вы́жить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to survive <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">continue to live</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to make someone leave (apartment, work or study place) by making their stay miserable or inconvenient, to squeeze (<i>transitive</i>)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***выжигать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a> (24491)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жига́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žigátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyžigátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжечь.html>вы́жечь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to burn out, to burn down, to scorch
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:клеймо.html>клеймо́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžigátʹ</b> klejmó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to brand</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжигать.html>выжига́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дерево.html>де́реву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžigátʹ</b> po dérevu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to do poker-work</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">medicine</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cauterize</li></ol>

***выжидать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжидать.html>выжида́ть</a> (14247)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жида́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-židátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжидать.html>выжида́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyžidátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выждать.html>вы́ждать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bide one's time, to wait <i>(for)</i>, to wait till something is over
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжидать.html>выжида́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удобный.html>удо́бного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:случай.html>слу́чая</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžidátʹ</b> udóbnovo slúčaja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wait for an opportunity</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***выжимать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a> (14128)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жима́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-žimátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">vyžimátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжать.html>вы́жать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to squeeze out, to press out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>сок</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лимон.html>лимо́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> sok iz limóna</i> ― <span class="e-translation">squeeze juice out of a lemon</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сок.html>со́ки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> sóki</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to sweat someone, to drive someone hard</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to wring (a cloth, etc.)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wring out, to get out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:возможный.html>возмо́жное</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> vsjó vozmóžnoje</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the most</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:максимальный.html>максима́льную</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:скорость.html>ско́рость</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ля</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> maksimálʹnuju skórostʹ iz avtomobílja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make the most mileage out of one's car</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:информация.html>информа́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> informáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to wring information</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжимать.html>выжима́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:улыбка.html>улы́бку</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>vyžimátʹ</b> iz sebjá ulýbku</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to force a smile</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sports</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to press, to lift (a weight)</li>
<li>to step on, to press on (the clutch, etc.)</li></ol>

</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span> применяя моральное давление, получать от кого-то информацию <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span> с трудом использовать последние ресурсы, силы <span class="example-fullblock example-absent-block"><ul>
</ul></li>


<li>медленным, нерезким усилием поднимать тяжесть на максимально возможную высоту или отодвигать на максимальное расстояние от себя <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Спортсмен легко <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">выжимает</span> левой рукой три пуда. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>

***выжить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:выжить.html>вы́жить</a> (3521)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы́-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vý-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:жить.html>жить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">žitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выжить.html>вы́жить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výžitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:выживать.html>выжива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to survive <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">continue to live</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make someone leave (an apartment, work or study place) by making their stay miserable or inconvenient, to squeeze out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">бара́шкин <a href = vnd.unilang:всячески.html>вся́чески</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́лся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:выжить.html>вы́жить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:блиндаж.html>блиндажа́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:переводчик.html>перево́дчика</a> ле́вина.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Baráškin vsjáčeski starálsja <b>výžitʹ</b> iz blindažá perevódčika Lévina.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Barashkin tried in every way to <b>squeeze</b> interpreter Levin from the dug-out.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́званный</a> (634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́званный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výzvannyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>generated, caused</li>
<li>aroused, renewed, touched</li>
<li>called, summoned</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звать</a> (634)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">вы-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vy-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:звать.html>зва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вызвать.html>вы́звать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">výzvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вызывать.html>вызыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to call, to send for</li>
<li>to challenge, to defy</li>
<li>to summon</li>
<li>to arouse, to cause, to evoke, to excite</li></ol>
